USE r2r;

SET FOREIGN_KEY_CHECKS = 0;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS ref_and_igdt;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS recipe_igdt;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS heart;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS rcp_and_seq;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS reviews;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS fridge;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS ingredients;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS recipes;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS member;

SET FOREIGN_KEY_CHECKS = 1;

SET FOREIGN_KEY_CHECKS = 0;

CREATE TABLE member (
    user_email VARCHAR(255) PRIMARY KEY,
    user_name VARCHAR(30) NOT NULL,
    user_pw VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    user_phone VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL
);

CREATE TABLE ingredients (
    igdt_id BIGINT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    igdt_name VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE
);

CREATE TABLE recipes (
    rcp_id BIGINT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    rcp_name VARCHAR(50),
    rcp_cooking_time VARCHAR(7),
    rcp_difficulty VARCHAR(10),
    rcp_image_URL VARCHAR(255),
    rcp_quantities VARCHAR(10)
);

CREATE TABLE fridge (
    rf_id BIGINT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    user_email VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE,
    FOREIGN KEY (user_email) REFERENCES member(user_email)
);

CREATE TABLE ref_and_igdt (
    ref_igdt_id BIGINT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    rf_id BIGINT,
    igdt_id BIGINT,
    purchase_date TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (igdt_id) REFERENCES ingredients(igdt_id),
    FOREIGN KEY (rf_id) REFERENCES fridge(rf_id)
);

CREATE TABLE recipe_igdt (
    rcp_igdt_id BIGINT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    rcp_id BIGINT,
    igdt_id BIGINT,
    rcp_igdt_amount VARCHAR(50),
    FOREIGN KEY (igdt_id) REFERENCES ingredients(igdt_id),
    FOREIGN KEY (rcp_id) REFERENCES recipes(rcp_id)
);

CREATE TABLE heart (
    fav_id BIGINT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    user_email VARCHAR(255),
    rcp_id BIGINT,
    FOREIGN KEY (user_email) REFERENCES member(user_email),
    FOREIGN KEY (rcp_id) REFERENCES recipes(rcp_id),
    UNIQUE (user_email, rcp_id)
);

CREATE TABLE rcp_and_seq (
    step_id BIGINT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    rcp_id BIGINT,
    step_number INT,
    step_description TEXT,
    step_url VARCHAR(255),
    FOREIGN KEY (rcp_id) REFERENCES recipes(rcp_id)
);

CREATE TABLE reviews (
    rv_id BIGINT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    user_email VARCHAR(255),
    rcp_id BIGINT,
    rating INT CHECK (rating >= 0 AND rating <= 5),
    comment TEXT,
    modified_date TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (user_email) REFERENCES member(user_email),
    FOREIGN KEY (rcp_id) REFERENCES recipes(rcp_id),
    UNIQUE (user_email, rcp_id)
);

SET FOREIGN_KEY_CHECKS = 1;
